import {
  GraphResultSet,
  RemoteJoinerOptions,
  RemoteQueryFunction,
  RemoteQueryInput,
} from "@medusajs/framework/types"
import { createStep, StepFunction, StepResponse } from "@medusajs/workflows-sdk"
import { ContainerRegistrationKeys } from "@medusajs/utils"

export type UseQueryGraphStepInput<
  TEntry extends string,
  TIsList extends boolean = boolean
> = RemoteQueryInput<TEntry> & {
  options?: RemoteJoinerOptions & {
    isList?: TIsList
  }
}

export type UseQueryGraphStepOutput<
  TEntry extends string,
  TIsList extends boolean = boolean
> = ReturnType<
  StepFunction<
    any,
    true extends TIsList
      ? GraphResultSet<TEntry>
      : Omit<GraphResultSet<TEntry>, "data"> & {
          data: GraphResultSet<TEntry>["data"][number]
        }
  >
>

const useQueryGraphStepId = "use-query-graph-step"

const step = createStep(
  useQueryGraphStepId,
  async (input: UseQueryGraphStepInput<any>, { container }) => {
    const query = container.resolve<RemoteQueryFunction>(
      ContainerRegistrationKeys.QUERY
    )

    const isList = input.options?.isList ?? true
    delete input.options?.isList

    const { options, ...queryConfig } = input

    const result = await query.graph(queryConfig as any, options)

    if (!isList) {
      const data = result.data?.[0]
      result.data = data
      return new StepResponse(result)
    }

    return new StepResponse(result)
  }
)

import {
  ContainerRegistrationKeys,
  Modules,
  PromotionActions,
} from "@medusajs/framework/utils"
import { StepResponse, createStep } from "@medusajs/framework/workflows-sdk"

/**
 * The details of the promotion codes to apply on a cart.
 */
export interface UpdateCartPromotionStepInput {
  /**
   * The ID of the cart to update promotions for.
   */
  id: string
  /**
   * The promotion codes to apply on the cart.
   */
  promo_codes?: string[]
  /**
   * Whether to add, remove, or replace promotion codes.
   */
  action?:
    | PromotionActions.ADD
    | PromotionActions.REMOVE
    | PromotionActions.REPLACE
}

export const updateCartPromotionsStepId = "update-cart-promotions"
/**
 * This step updates the promotions applied on a cart.
 */
export const updateCartPromotionsStep = createStep(
  updateCartPromotionsStepId,
  async (data: UpdateCartPromotionStepInput, { container }) => {
    const { promo_codes = [], id, action = PromotionActions.ADD } = data

    const remoteLink = container.resolve(ContainerRegistrationKeys.LINK)
    const remoteQuery = container.resolve(
      ContainerRegistrationKeys.REMOTE_QUERY
    )

    const existingCartPromotionLinks = await remoteQuery({
      entryPoint: "cart_promotion",
      fields: ["cart_id", "promotion_id"],
      variables: {
        cart_id: [id],
      },
    })

    const promotionLinkMap = new Map<string, any>(
      existingCartPromotionLinks.map((link) => [link.promotion_id, link])
    )

    const linksToCreate: any[] = []
    const linksToDismiss: any[] = []

    if (promo_codes?.length) {
      const query = container.resolve(ContainerRegistrationKeys.QUERY)
      const { data: promotions } = await query.graph(
        {
          entity: "promotion",
          fields: ["id", "code"],
          filters: { code: promo_codes },
        },
        {
          cache: {
            enable: true,
          },
        }
      )

      for (const promotion of promotions) {
        const linkObject = {
          [Modules.CART]: { cart_id: id },
          [Modules.PROMOTION]: { promotion_id: promotion.id },
        }

        if ([PromotionActions.ADD, PromotionActions.REPLACE].includes(action)) {
          linksToCreate.push(linkObject)
        }

        if (action === PromotionActions.REMOVE) {
          const link = promotionLinkMap.get(promotion.id)

          if (link) {
            linksToDismiss.push(linkObject)
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (action === PromotionActions.REPLACE) {
      for (const link of existingCartPromotionLinks) {
        linksToDismiss.push({
          [Modules.CART]: { cart_id: link.cart_id },
          [Modules.PROMOTION]: { promotion_id: link.promotion_id },
        })
      }
    }

    if (linksToDismiss.length) {
      await remoteLink.dismiss(linksToDismiss)
    }

    const createdLinks = linksToCreate.length
      ? await remoteLink.create(linksToCreate)
      : []

    return new StepResponse(null, {
 *

 *   }]

 */

import { updateCartPromotionsWorkflow } from "@medusajs/core-flows"
import { medusaIntegrationTestRunner } from "@medusajs/test-utils"
import {
  ICartModuleService,
  ICustomerModuleService,
  IOrderModuleService,
  IPromotionModuleService,
} from "@medusajs/types"
import {
  CampaignBudgetType,
  Modules,
  OrderStatus,
  PromotionActions,
  PromotionStatus,
  PromotionType,
} from "@medusajs/utils"
import {
  adminHeaders,
  createAdminUser,
} from "../../../../helpers/create-admin-user"

jest.setTimeout(100000)

const env = {}

medusaIntegrationTestRunner({
  env,
  testSuite: ({ dbConnection, getContainer }) => {
    describe("First-order promotions", () => {
      let appContainer
      let cartModule: ICartModuleService
      let customerModule: ICustomerModuleService
      let orderModule: IOrderModuleService
      let promotionModule: IPromotionModuleService

      beforeAll(async () => {
        appContainer = getContainer()
        cartModule = appContainer.resolve(Modules.CART)
        customerModule = appContainer.resolve(Modules.CUSTOMER)
        orderModule = appContainer.resolve(Modules.ORDER)
        promotionModule = appContainer.resolve(Modules.PROMOTION)
      })

      beforeEach(async () => {
        await createAdminUser(dbConnection, adminHeaders, appContainer)
      })

      const createCustomer = async (email: string) => {
        return await customerModule.createCustomers({ email })
      }

      const createCart = async (customerId?: string) => {
        return await cartModule.createCarts({
          currency_code: "usd",
          customer_id: customerId,
          items: [
            {
              unit_price: 2000,
              quantity: 1,
              title: "Test item",
              product_id: "prod_test",
            } as any,
          ],
        })
      }

      const createFirstOrderPromotion = async (
        code: string,
        extra: Record<string, any> = {}
      ) => {
        return await promotionModule.createPromotions({
          code,
          type: PromotionType.STANDARD,
          status: PromotionStatus.ACTIVE,
          rules: [
            {
              attribute: "customer.has_completed_order",
              operator: "eq",
              values: ["false"],
            },
          ],
          application_method: {
            type: "fixed",
            target_type: "items",
            allocation: "across",
            value: 500,
            apply_to_quantity: 1,
            currency_code: "usd",
          },
          ...extra,
        })
      }

      const createHistoricalOrder = async (
        customerId: string,
        status: OrderStatus,
        isDraftOrder = false
      ) => {
        return await orderModule.createOrders({
          status,
          customer_id: customerId,
          email: `${customerId}@example.com`,
          currency_code: "usd",
          is_draft_order: isDraftOrder,
          items: [
            {
              title: "Historical item",
              quantity: 1,
              unit_price: 1000,
            },
          ],
        } as any)
      }

      const applyPromotion = async (cartId: string, code: string) => {
        await updateCartPromotionsWorkflow(appContainer).run({
          input: {
            cart_id: cartId,
            promo_codes: [code],
            action: PromotionActions.ADD,
          },
        })

        return await cartModule.retrieveCart(cartId, {
          relations: ["items", "items.adjustments"],
        })
      }

      it("applies only for customers without completed historical orders", async () => {
        const customer = await createCustomer("first-order@example.com")
        const promotion = await createFirstOrderPromotion("FIRST_ORDER_ONLY")
        const cart = await createCart(customer.id)

        const updatedCart = await applyPromotion(cart.id, promotion.code!)

        expect(updatedCart.items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual(
          expect.arrayContaining([
            expect.objectContaining({
              code: promotion.code,
              amount: 500,
            }),
          ])
        )
      })

      it("does not apply for missing customers or customers with completed historical orders", async () => {
        const customer = await createCustomer("returning@example.com")
        await createHistoricalOrder(customer.id, OrderStatus.COMPLETED)
        const promotion = await createFirstOrderPromotion("RETURNING_BLOCKED")

        const returningCart = await createCart(customer.id)
        const guestCart = await createCart()

        const updatedReturningCart = await applyPromotion(
          returningCart.id,
          promotion.code!
        )
        const updatedGuestCart = await applyPromotion(guestCart.id, promotion.code!)

        expect(updatedReturningCart.items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual([])
        expect(updatedGuestCart.items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual([])
      })

      it("ignores canceled, pending, and draft orders when checking first completed order", async () => {
        const customer = await createCustomer("status-edge@example.com")
        await createHistoricalOrder(customer.id, OrderStatus.CANCELED)
        await createHistoricalOrder(customer.id, OrderStatus.PENDING)
        await createHistoricalOrder(customer.id, OrderStatus.COMPLETED, true)

        const promotion = await createFirstOrderPromotion("STATUS_EDGE")
        const cart = await createCart(customer.id)

        const updatedCart = await applyPromotion(cart.id, promotion.code!)

        expect(updatedCart.items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual(
          expect.arrayContaining([
            expect.objectContaining({
              code: promotion.code,
              amount: 500,
            }),
          ])
        )
      })

      it("blocks exhausted global and per-customer caps and releases usage on revert", async () => {
        const customer = await createCustomer("caps@example.com")
        const globalPromotion = await createFirstOrderPromotion(
          "GLOBAL_CAP",
          {
            limit: 1,
            used: 1,
          }
        )
        const perCustomerPromotion = await createFirstOrderPromotion(
          "CUSTOMER_CAP",
          {
            campaign: {
              name: "Customer cap",
              campaign_identifier: "customer-cap",
              budget: {
                type: CampaignBudgetType.USE_BY_ATTRIBUTE,
                attribute: "customer_id",
                limit: 1,
              },
            },
          }
        )

        await promotionModule.registerUsage(
          [{ amount: 500, code: perCustomerPromotion.code! }],
          { customer_id: customer.id, customer_email: null }
        )

        const globalCart = await createCart(customer.id)
        const customerCart = await createCart(customer.id)

        expect((await applyPromotion(globalCart.id, globalPromotion.code!)).items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual([])
        expect((await applyPromotion(customerCart.id, perCustomerPromotion.code!)).items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual([])

        await promotionModule.revertUsage(
          [{ amount: 500, code: perCustomerPromotion.code! }],
          { customer_id: customer.id, customer_email: null }
        )

        const releasedCart = await createCart(customer.id)
        const updatedReleasedCart = await applyPromotion(
          releasedCart.id,
          perCustomerPromotion.code!
        )

        expect(updatedReleasedCart.items?.[0].adjustments).toEqual(
          expect.arrayContaining([
            expect.objectContaining({
              code: perCustomerPromotion.code,
              amount: 500,
            }),
          ])
        )
      })
    })
  },
})
